			<h1 class="ish-sc-element ish-sc_headline ish-color14 ish-center ish-no-margin"><span class="ish-icon ish-left"><span class="ish-icon-attention"></span></span>Cooling Centers open through Sunday, September 3rd</h1>
	<div class="wpb_text_column wpb_content_element  ish-text-color14" style="">
		<div class="wpb_wrapper">
			<p style="text-align: center;">The National Weather Service has forecasted that the temperature in Fresno will be at or above 105 degrees.<br />
As a result, all cooling centers will be open between 12 pm – 8 pm.</p>
